<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voznosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***превосходить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превосходить.html>превосходи́ть</a> (9208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пре-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pre-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:восходить.html>восходи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vosxodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превосходить.html>превосходи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevosxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превзойти.html>превзойти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to excel, to surpass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превосходить.html>превосходи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:численность.html>чи́сленностью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevosxodítʹ</b> číslennostʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to outnumber</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to surpass, to exceed</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превосходный.html>превосхо́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prevosxódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***превратиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превратиться.html>преврати́ться</a> (1640)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">прѣвратити сѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prěvratiti sę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet with native <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перевороти́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevorotítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратиться.html>преврати́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevratítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превращаться.html>превраща́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn into, to change into</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратить.html>преврати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***превратность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тность</a> (26539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">превра́тный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevrátnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevrátnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратность.html>превра́тностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vicissitude, changeability (a change, especially in one's life or fortunes)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменчивость.html>изме́нчивость</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izménčivostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">непостоянство</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nepostojanstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злоключение.html>злоключе́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zloključénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***превращать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превращать.html>превраща́ть</a> (6582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратить.html>преврати́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevratítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превращать.html>превраща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevraščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превратить.html>преврати́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn into, to change</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a> (11998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevýsitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exceed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:полномочие.html>полномо́чия</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevýsitʹ</b> vlastʹ / polnomóčija</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to exceed one's authority</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорость.html>ско́рость</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevýsitʹ</b> skórostʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to speed</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a> (4641)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prevýsitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevyšátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превысить.html>превы́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exceed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:власть.html>власть</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:полномочие.html>полномо́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevyšátʹ</b> vlastʹ / polnomóčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to exceed one's authority</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:превышать.html>превыша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорость.html>ско́рость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prevyšátʹ</b> skórostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to speed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***превыше.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:превыше.html>превы́ше</a> (19692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:превыше.html>превы́ше</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prevýše</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(+ genitive)</i> above
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спокойствие.html>споко́йствие</a> — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:превыше.html>превы́ше</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Spokójstvije — <b>prevýše</b> vsevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Serenity above all else</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:забота.html>забо́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ке</a> — <b><a href = vnd.unilang:превыше.html>превы́ше</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zabóta o čelovéke — <b>prevýše</b> vsevó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Service to mankind above all else</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="возвышенный стиль"><a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́к</a>.</span><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">, <a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>обы́чно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> сочет. <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:намного.html>намно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выше.html>вы́ше</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:гораздо.html>гора́здо</a> сильнее <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> важнее <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>

***предавать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предавать.html>предава́ть</a> (12341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">перда́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perdátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предавать.html>предава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предать.html>преда́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to betray</li>
<li>to expose, to subject, to commit, to hand over</li></ol>
